<div class="entry-content single-content">
	<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id1005_a12509-2e alignfull has-theme-palette9-background-color kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-row kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kb-theme-content-width">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column1005_0330c0-e1"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="kt-adv-heading1005_b11610-c7 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1005_b11610-c7">Finding Wholesome Books, One Page at a Time</div>



<h2 class="kt-adv-heading1005_1cae18-74 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1005_1cae18-74">Welcome to Fruitful Reader.</h2>



<p class="kt-adv-heading1005_28d990-df wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1005_28d990-df">Looking for your next favorite book? You&#8217;re in the right place. </p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading1005_3287f3-d8 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1005_3287f3-d8">Dive into handpicked recommendations and cozy up with a good read. Feels like a lazy afternoon with a hot drink and a great book, doesn&#8217;t it?</p>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column1005_d17fc9-03"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id1005_ed6fbd-07 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-3-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kb-theme-content-width">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column1005_ec5e7b-35"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<figure class="wp-block-kadence-image kb-image1005_d252fd-94 size-full kb-image-is-ratio-size"><a href="https://fruitfulreader.com/category/book-review/" class="kb-advanced-image-link"><div class="kb-is-ratio-image kb-image-ratio-square"><picture><source srcset="https://fruitfulreader.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/1.webp 819w,https://fruitfulreader.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/1-240x300.webp 240w,https://fruitfulreader.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/1-768x960.webp 768w" sizes="(max-width: 819px) 100vw, 819px" type="image/webp"><img src="https://fruitfulreader.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/1.png" height="1024" width="819" srcset="https://fruitfulreader.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/1.png 819w, https://fruitfulreader.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/1-240x300.png 240w, https://fruitfulreader.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/1-768x960.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 819px) 100vw, 819px" class="kb-img wp-image-4918 sp-no-webp" alt="" decoding="async"  > </picture></div></a></figure>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column1005_dab254-29 kb-section-has-link"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h5 class="kt-adv-heading1005_f95e21-b1 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1005_f95e21-b1"><a href="https://fruitfulreader.com/category/book-review/" data-type="link" data-id="https://fruitfulreader.com/category/book-review/">Book Reviews</a></h5>
</div><a href="https://fruitfulreader.com/category/book-review/" class="kb-section-link-overlay"></a></div>

<p class="kt-adv-heading69944_859e99-6d wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading69944_859e99-6d">If you’re as passionate about reading as I am, why not take the next step and join my exclusive Facebook group, the <strong>Clean &amp; Christian Readers Book Club</strong>? </p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading69944_1de804-fd wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading69944_1de804-fd">It&#8217;s the perfect place to dive deeper into your literary journey, get personalized book recommendations, and share your favorite reads with a supportive community.</p>

<h4 class="kt-adv-heading1005_9e2434-57 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-2-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1005_9e2434-57"><em>Hi there!</em></h4>



<h2 class="kt-adv-heading1005_e64584-1a wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1005_e64584-1a">I&#8217;m Kassidy Griffin,</h2>



<p>The proud founder of Fruitful Reader. I&#8217;ve been burying my nose in books since 2004 and, let me tell you, I&#8217;ve gone through thousands of them across all genres. </p>



<p>You can catch me reading pretty much every single day. Since starting Fruitful Reader, I&#8217;ve had the joy of helping countless women discover wholesome, clean, and spiritually uplifting books.</p>



<p>I&#8217;m on a bit of a mission, you see. I want to assist you in finding your next favorite book. Can&#8217;t wait to get started, can you?</p>

<h2 class="kt-adv-heading1005_ef8dbe-30 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1005_ef8dbe-30">Cozy Escape Book Club</h2>



<p class="kt-adv-heading1005_eb2d7a-7c wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1005_eb2d7a-7c">Only $9, a month</p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading1005_0a44d3-22 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1005_0a44d3-22">Finally, a book club that feels like a retreat.</p>



<p><br>No more pretending to love what “everyone” else is reading. Here, you’ll find stories that make you smile, friends who get you, and space to slow down.</p>



<p>This book club is your instant retreat where books, joyful conversations, and community all come together. It’s the self-care your busy life has been missing.</p>
